Wang Kemin Discusses Huang Fu's Firm Resignation 99

Huang's Condition Has Recovered and He Plans to Go to Shanghai in the Coming Days

Hangzhou Correspondence: Wang Kemin, the former Acting Chairman of the Beiping Political Readjustment Committee, arrived in Hangzhou with his wife and daughter on the afternoon of the 28th. He rested at the Bank of China villa on Shengtang Road. In the evening, he was feted by Jin Runquan, the manager of the Hangzhou branch of the Bank of China, and then stayed at the Bank of China villa. At 8:00 a.m. on the 29th, he and Yu Jiaji, the former secretary-general of the Beiping Political Readjustment Committee, took a car to Mogan Mountain to meet Huang Fu, reporting on the conclusion of the Beiping Political Readjustment Committee. In the afternoon, he returned to Hangzhou from Mogan Mountain at 5:30 p.m. In the evening, Mayor Zhou Xiangxian of Hangzhou specially held a banquet at Lou Wai Lou on West Lake for Wang and his wife, as well as Cheng Tianfang, the newly appointed ambassador to Germany, and his wife, who came to Hangzhou for sightseeing. Those present to accompany them included Xu Qingfu, Jin Runquan, and Yu Shaosong. The gathering broke up at 9:00 p.m. Yesterday (1st) at 8:00 a.m., Wang and his wife went to Battery Hill and Liuxia and other places to sweep the graves and search for a burial site for his wife. It was decided that Wang's wife will govern the funeral affairs, staying for half a month, and then transport the coffin south for burial. According to Wang, he went to Mogan Mountain yesterday to meet Huang Yingbai to report on the conclusion of the Beiping Political Readjustment Committee. Huang's illness has greatly recovered, but his nasal breathing is not yet fully clear, and his left arm can move quite freely and can untie the buckles under his ribs himself. Huang expressed his intention to go down the mountain to Shanghai in the coming days, perhaps to have a medical check-up. His intention to resign from the position of Minister of Interior is still firm, and he has no intention of taking office. The reporter also visited Yu Jiaji at Room 42 of the Xinxin Hotel and inquired about the current situation in North China. According to him, after the conclusion of the Beiping Political Readjustment Committee, the foreign affairs of Hebei, those concerning local matters are the responsibility of the provincial government, and major matters are handled directly by the central government. The current situation in North China is good. If the local authorities handle matters properly, branch problems may not arise. The counties in the war zone are the responsibility of the commissioners of Ji and Mi and the county magistrates, because Koreans and Chinese live together, making it more difficult to deal with. The Hebei Economic Association is organized by people from the business and banking sectors and is planning to improve and adjust the local economy. Government personnel have not participated. Mr. Shulu's future whereabouts are uncertain. After Song Zheyuan took office as the commander of the Tianjin Garrison, he had harmonious relations with all parties, and there were no problems with local appeals. He met with He Yingqin many times in Nanjing, but his return to the north is not yet scheduled. He has not had time to return to his hometown for four years. This time, he took time to come to Hangzhou and will return to his original residence in Shaoxing to take care of personal matters, staying for a day or two, and then go to Shanghai, pass through Nanjing, and return to the north. President Wang entrusted Mr. Wang Shulu to urge Mr. Huang Yingbai to go to Nanjing as soon as possible to take up the position of Minister of Interior, but Huang still intends to rest for a while, and there is no preparation for taking office at present. (October 1st)

Current Situation of the Sulfuric Acid Plant in Guangdong Province 100

Daily Output of Fifteen Tons

Guangzhou Correspondence: Since Guangdong Province implemented the Three-Year Administrative Plan, it has built 24 major factories to actively develop industry. Due to the fact that sulfuric acid is an industrial raw material, it was specially prepared in advance and established in July of the year before last, costing more than 890,000 yuan. The director of the factory is Huang Bingfang, who studied chemistry in the United States and is very experienced. Therefore, the factory's products have achieved excellent results. They have been repeatedly tested by various chemists, all of whom believe that the quality is pure and comparable to imported products. The price is more than half lower than imported products, so industrial manufacturers are happy to purchase them. The current daily output is 15 tons, and the monthly output is 450 tons. In the year since its establishment, it has produced more than 10,000 tons. In addition, the Guangdong Textile Factory's adjacent fertilizer factory has been established one after another, and the paper mill is also in preparation. Sulfuric acid has a wider range of uses, and the factory is actively planning to expand and increase production to meet supply and demand. As for raw materials, it initially relied on imports, but now the province can supply itself.

Songjiang - County Magistrate Jin's Resignation Approved

Our County Magistrate Jin Tigan has been in Songjiang for three years. Recently, he suddenly felt negative and submitted a request to the province to resign and return to his original occupation. The letter of resignation was submitted more than a month ago, and there was no news for a long time, resulting in many rumors. Now we have received news from the province that the provincial government meeting on the 1st approved County Magistrate Jin's resignation, and Li Qia, the county magistrate of Tiansha County, has been transferred to fill the vacancy. It is said that County Magistrate Li has held many busy positions and has a good reputation for his administration. Being transferred to the management of Songjiang is an easy task and is truly a blessing for the people of Songjiang.

Changshu - A Large Quantity of Opium Discovered on the Riverbank

Li Xiaomei and two other villagers from Mawan Township in the Sixth District discovered a large quantity of opium on the riverbank of Yemaokou yesterday morning. They reported it to the town's patrol ship, which then opened the packages for inspection. The packages contained 32 catties (more than 1,500 taels) of private opium, all wrapped in cotton and made into two packages, like bedding. It has now been sealed together with the township head and others and sent to the county government. It is said that Jiangbian in Yemaokou often has river boats passing through it. It is rumored that this opium was purchased privately by opium traffickers and was waiting for delivery at the mouth. This time, it was discovered because the timing was not accurate, resulting in the cracking of the case.

Local News

Central Trust Bureau Opened Yesterday Morning, Kong Reported on the Purpose of Establishment and Business Policy, First Board of Directors Meeting Was Held to Discuss Ongoing Matters, Another 5 Million Yuan Was Allocated to Establish the Central Savings Association 101

The Central Trust Bureau, which has been in preparation for more than a year, was formally established at 9:00 a.m. yesterday and held an opening ceremony. Kong Xiangxi, the Minister of Finance, Governor of the Central Bank, and Chairman of the Bureau, attended the ceremony in person and gave instructions. The ceremony was grand, and about a thousand people from all sectors of China and abroad went to congratulate, making it a grand occasion for a while. The details of each situation are recorded as follows:

Visiting Guests

Those who went to congratulate from all sectors of China and abroad, in addition to the Chairman of the Bureau Kong Xiangxi, Standing Directors Zhang Jia'ao and Guo Zhuotang, Directors Song Ziliang and Xu Kan, Supervisors Chen Xing, Li Ming, and Chen Guangfu, included Wu Tiecheng, Tang Shoumin, Qian Xinzhi, Du Yuesheng, Zhou Zongliang, Li Fuxun, Xu Jiying, Hu Mengjia, Song Hanzhang, Wang Yansong, Wang Boyuan, Zhu Boquan, Zhao Tiezhang, Yang Hu, Wang Zhinan, Zeng Rongfu, Jiang Lufu, Wang Xiaolai, Yu Zuoting, Dai Mingli, Chen Bilin, Bella Seem, Ma Shaoqing, Chen Liting, Liu Hongsheng, Chen Aishi, Nie Lusheng, Zhao Jinqing, Zheng Hongnian, Heck Quimen, Mackay, and more than a thousand people. The Director and Deputy Director of the Bureau and all staff warmly welcomed them and served tea and snacks.

Opening Ceremony

At the entrance of the bureau at 126 Hankou Road, the Party and national flags were crossed left and right, and decorated with pine, cypress, and fresh flowers. All the staff wore red silk flowers, full of a new atmosphere. At 8:00 a.m., Chinese and foreign guests began to arrive one after another, and were warmly welcomed by the Director and Deputy Director of the Bureau and the staff, and led to visit various places. The auditorium was located in the conference hall on the third floor, with a portrait of Sun Yat-sen and Party and national flags hanging in the middle. The surrounding area was decorated with flower baskets, silver shields, and silver tripods presented by various sectors. At 9:00 a.m. sharp, the opening ceremony was held, the ceremony was simple and grand, and the Director, Deputy Director, and all managers and directors of the bureau, and all staff gathered in the auditorium. First, Zhang Jia'ao, Vice Governor of the Bank of China and Director of the Bureau, delivered a speech, followed by Chairman Kong Xiangxi. The ceremony ended at half past nine.

Director's Instructions

Director Zhang Jia'ao, who is also the Vice Governor, gave a speech, briefly saying that today is the official establishment of the Central Trust Bureau. After more than a year of preparation by Director Ye Zhuotang and others, and the thorough planning of Minister Kong, today's great cause was established. At this time of economic decline, Minister Kong resolutely organized the establishment of the Central Trust Bureau to promote savings and provide trust services to the country and society. His great spirit is truly admired by his colleagues. Today, Minister Kong came in person and will announce to his colleagues the motives for establishing the trust bureau and the great policies for the future.

Minister's Instructions

Chairman Kong Xiangxi, also Governor of the Central Bank, said in his instructions, briefly, that he was very happy to meet everyone today. The Central Trust Bureau has been in preparation for more than a year. Due to various reasons and the location of the bureau, it was delayed until today before it was officially established. Why did the central government want to establish the Central Trust Bureau? Because there are many events on the government side that need to be entrusted to a commercial institution for management. At the same time, the Central Bank is limited to the status of a national bank and acts as the national treasury, which is inconvenient in fact and in procedure. Therefore, a trust business independent agency was specially organized under the Central Bank to undertake all the affairs of the trust bureau, to handle various trusts and insurances, and to promote savings. The motive for promoting savings is not only commercial, but also has important political relations. The state has considerable guarantees for civil servants, such as future retirement, or in the event of an accident during the service period, and the payment of condolence money, so that they can be held responsible for their duties. The Ministry of Finance has regulations on this, such as bonuses and retirement money from the customs. The idea is to make every civil servant work hard for the public and must first settle his family, so that he has no worries. This matter was discussed with Chairman Chiang, who greatly agreed and advocated that the armed forces should also be promoted. Therefore, the bureau has the establishment of military savings, but savings are not limited to civil servants and armed forces, but also need to be expanded to the social sector. Therefore, other savings must be gradually handled in the future. However, the bureau was established by the government and should not compete with merchants for profit. As for the insurance business, the scope is not very large now, so I will not go into details. However, creating a business in the world is not only possible with organization, but also requires people to execute it, so every organization needs people to do it. The Central Trust Bureau is not only a commercial organization, but can be said to be very meaningful for the national construction plan. As the name suggests, if it cannot be done in practice, it will affect the Trust Bureau in the future. It has a great relationship and responsibility to the country and the nation. Because all people do things, first trust and then entrust. Not only must major entrustments be handled with caution, but also minor matters must be handled strictly. Today I advise my colleagues, no matter what, do not forget the word "trust", not only should you encourage yourself in official business, but also pay attention to your personal morality. And doing things is not in the size of the position, for example, building tall buildings, the materials of the beams and pillars are certainly necessary, but the connection depends on the strength of small nails, otherwise the doors and trees cannot be connected, and the building cannot be completed. Therefore, whether it is a senior or junior staff, everyone must work hard, do not think that the Trust Bureau is founded by the central government and has abundant capital, and waste everything casually and do things casually. You must know that the prosperity and decline of the country is every closely related to the diligence, frugality, extravagance, and laziness of the people. For example, our neighbor to the east, which can dominate the world, is due to the hard work of its people. If every one of us is hardworking and cautious, the country and the nation will have the hope of rejuvenation. The ancients said that everyone is responsible for the rise and fall of the country. At this time of national crisis, I hope that my colleagues will pay attention. You must know that this bureau is a cause with great significance. In the future, you must be cautious in everything you encounter. Director Zhang's past spirit of doing things is admirable. I entrusted you with the responsibility of developing construction with mobile finance. I hope that you will all show your strengths, work hard, and develop the inherent spirit of the Chinese nation.

Meeting of Directors and Supervisors

After the opening ceremony, a meeting of directors and supervisors was held at 9:45 a.m. Those present included Chairman Kong Xiangxi, Standing Directors Zhang Jia'ao and Guo Zhuotang, Directors Song Ziliang and Xu Kan, Supervisors Chen Xing, Li Ming, and Chen Guangfu. Chairman Kong Xiangxi presided over the meeting. During the meeting, the business policy and other matters were discussed in detail, and the meeting adjourned at 10:30 a.m.

Savings Announcement

Central Trust Bureau Announcement No. 2 says that the bureau was specially authorized by the National Government's order on August of the 24th year of the Republic to establish the Central Savings Association to handle savings matters such as monthly lotteries for bonus repayment and interest payment. The bureau has now allocated 5 million yuan of national currency as the fund of the association to handle the savings business with independent accounting, and a supervisory committee has been set up to review the use of funds. Except for the date of commencement of business, which will be determined and announced in detail, this announcement is made.

Martyr Huang Yuquan - Monument Unveiling Held Yesterday at Hongqiao Airfield 102

The China Aviation Association, to commemorate Martyr Huang Yuquan's sacrifice on January 28th, raised funds from its directors to build a monument at Hongqiao. Yesterday at 3 PM, the unveiling ceremony was held. Attendees included Mayor Wu Tiecheng, Aviation Association Chairman Wang Xiaolai, Secretary-General Yao Xijiu, Directors Li Dachao, Zeng Yijing, Nie Kaiyi, Solicitation Team Leaders Lin Genghou, Wu Qiding, and others. Prominent figures from society, the China Flying Club's Yang Guozhu and Zhu Dong, the Central Relief Committee's Huang Bodu, representatives from Hangzhou Aviation School (Shi You and Chen Jia'ao), Naval Shipyard Director Ma De, Ningbo-France Association's Wu Qilin, Water Disaster Relief Association, Xinwei Relief Association, and other organizations, totaling over a hundred people. The China Aviation Association dispatched Chen Chengzhi, Zhou Junde, Zhang Yuliang, Chen Shuo, Lou Shengyang, Bao Lengxue, Li Jimin, and others to arrange the reception. Mayor Wu presided over the meeting, Chen Shuo gave a memorial address, and Huang Jun served as master of ceremonies. Details are as follows:

Chairman's Report

Chairman Mayor Wu reported, briefly stating, "Distinguished guests, today is the unveiling ceremony for the Martyr Huang Yuquan Monument. Martyr Huang sacrificed himself at Hongqiao on January 28th. The China Aviation Association, to commemorate the martyr, built this monument here. Life and death are commonplace, but some deaths are heavier than Mount Tai, while others are lighter than a feather. Martyr Huang, in his prime, during the most precious time of his life, was able to sacrifice himself for the country and the nation. This death is extremely valuable. Though dead, he still lives on. Martyr Huang was an aviator and an air force officer. He aspired to be an aerial warrior. His sacrifice for the country and the nation during the January 28th Incident is truly regrettable. However, we, the survivors, to recognize merit and repay virtue, built this monument to commemorate and never forget. We deeply hope that all people of the nation and ambitious youth can emulate this spirit of patriotic fervor and strive for the survival of the country and the nation, so that the future will hold boundless hope."

Biographical Sketch

Following this, Aviation Association Chairman Wang Xiaolai reported on Martyr Huang's biographical sketch, saying, "Martyr Huang Yuquan was a native of Guangdong, born in the United States seven years before the founding of the Republic. His brother, Mr. Yupei, also grew up in the United States. After completing his studies, he served as a professor at the US Tites Aviation School. Martyr Huang, inspired by his brother, aspired to learn aviation and serve his motherland. Therefore, after graduating from middle school, he entered Tites Aviation School to study both flight and mechanical engineering. In the fifteenth year of the Republic, he returned to China and became a pilot. The following year, the martyr was dispatched to Russia to study military aviation, further deepening his knowledge. He then returned to China to serve, successively holding positions such as Chief of Flight Inspection, Senior Flight Mechanical Instructor, and Squadron Leader and Deputy Squadron Leader in the aviation team. He devoted himself to his duties and achieved outstanding results. Over several years, the nation faced numerous events. The martyr was ordered to rush to Guangdong, Guangxi, Shandong, Anhui, Shaanxi, and Henan, participating in almost every campaign. In the early spring of the twenty-first year, the martyr took leave from the north to return south and marry Miss He Qiaosheng in Guangzhou. Before a week had passed, the January 28th Incident occurred. His brother, Mr. Yupei, then serving as the captain of the Sixth Aviation Team, led his family to Shanghai. The martyr also came from Guangdong. On February 5th, he received orders to depart. At Hongqiao Airfield, he bravely took the lead. Suddenly, the aircraft was damaged, and the martyr died in service. Previously, due to mechanical failures, he had been forced to land, damaging the aircraft. However, the martyr, using his extraordinary skills, had always survived. Was it not heaven's will to fulfill his ambition to save the country through aviation and bestow upon him the honor of sacrificing himself for the nation? Saving the nation through aviation was Premier Sun Yat-sen's instruction. Martyr Huang Yuquan died implementing this instruction. Our China Aviation Association was also established to realize this instruction. Therefore, on January 15th of this year, during a board meeting, Director Zhang Hui proposed that a monument be erected to commemorate Martyr Huang Yuquan, who died in service at Hongqiao Airfield during the January 28th Incident. This was resolved and the association initiated the monument construction, entrusting Directors Zhang Hui, Yao Xijiu, and Hu Junzhuang to plan the project. Later, the Aviation Committee designated a location next to the Xiao De monument at Hongqiao Airfield for the martyr's monument. Association directors were responsible for fundraising, and the China Stone Company undertook the construction. Now, the monument is completed. The inscription on the monument was written by Chairman Lin of the National Government. The biographical sketch was written by Director Zhang Hui, and the inscription was drafted by myself. The calligraphy was done by Mayor Wu and Association Directors Wang Zhengting, Lin Kanghou, and Chen Qingyun – all dedicated to saving the country through aviation. Today, we hold this unveiling ceremony. Your presence and participation signify your shared sentiment. The martyr's illustrious name will forever endure with this monument."

Family Response

The martyr's brother, Huang Yupei, currently serving as the principal of the Luoyang branch of the Central Aviation School, also attended to represent the family and give a brief response, saying, "My younger brother, Yuquan, died for the country, fulfilling a duty that the people are willing to undertake. The China Aviation Association erected this monument, and today, we hold this unveiling ceremony. I am grateful for the presence of representatives from all sectors. I feel deeply saddened but also express my gratitude. During the January 28th Incident, my younger brother served as the deputy captain of the Sixth Aviation Team. Angered by the national crisis, he bravely took the lead. Despite being outnumbered, he engaged in combat and suffered severe injuries, sacrificing himself in service on February 5th. My younger brother's death for the country is not to be regretted. I hope that my fellow countrymen will pay attention to the construction of the air force so that we can achieve the goal of resisting foreign aggression and ensuring our survival in the future," etc. The meeting adjourned at 5 PM.

Opium Addicts' Voluntary Registration - Approved Extension of One Month 109

Compulsory Registration to be Implemented from November 1st

The Shanghai Public Safety Bureau was ordered to handle the voluntary registration period for opium addicts, which was originally scheduled to end on September 30th. However, due to the short period, some opium addicts were unable to register on time. The bureau has now obtained approval from the municipal government to allow opium addicts to continue to register voluntarily during the first month (i.e., October) of the compulsory registration period, without being fined, to show leniency. From November 1st, the decision was made to implement compulsory registration and impose penalties according to regulations. The bureau issued a public notice to the citizens on September 30th, which stated: "It has been over two months since this bureau began implementing the registration of opium addicts. We have repeatedly instructed our subordinates to conduct door-to-door persuasion. The number of opium addicts who have voluntarily come to register has been quite enthusiastic. The deadline for voluntary registration has now passed. From October to the end of December, it will be the compulsory registration period. During this period, if any opium addicts are found to be concealing themselves, once discovered by this bureau, they should be punished according to Article 4 of the 'Measures for Registering Opium Addicts During the Compulsory Period,' which provides for a fine of fifty yuan up to three hundred yuan. They will then be forced to register. However, considering that the registration period for opium addicts in this city is short, some opium addicts are unclear about the registration procedures and are hesitant to register, so the number of those who have not come to the bureau for voluntary registration on time is not small. If we do not leniently give them an opportunity to confess, and punish them all, it would be contrary to the government's intention to protect the citizens. This bureau has submitted a request to the municipal government, which has been approved under Instruction No. 3177, to allow opium addicts to register voluntarily during the first month (i.e., October) of the compulsory registration period. If, after repeated persuasion, there are still those who stubbornly resist and disobey, they will be detained and forced to register, but they will not be fined, to show leniency. From November 1st, this bureau will strictly investigate and implement compulsory registration, and impose penalties according to regulations, in order to complete the registration of opium addicts by the end of this year. This extension of the voluntary registration period is the final deadline. Opium addicts will no longer have the opportunity to confess. They should all be aware of the severity of the law and the urgency of the situation, and encourage each other to come to the bureau to register. If there are still those who are hesitant and delay, and are unwilling to come forward voluntarily, after the end of October, they will be detained and severely punished according to the law, without any leniency. Let all comply without fail. This is a public notice."

Summary of Benefits to Farmland from the Min Sheng Canal in Qi County, Henan 112

The Chinese Jiesheng Association, considering the Min Sheng Canal in Qi County, Henan, to be the county's largest water conservancy project, allocated 10,000 yuan from its charity funds in the autumn of the 18th year of the Republic to repair the canal, which could irrigate over 1,000 hectares. In recent years, various places have suffered from major droughts and floods, but the county has achieved bumper harvests. This was previously reported in the newspaper. Now, the association has received a letter from Liu Junye, Chairman of the Min Sheng Canal Management Committee in Qi County, reporting that, according to the investigators, the 1,000 hectares of land irrigated by the canal this year have yielded over 20,000 more shi of grain in the spring and autumn seasons compared to previous years, worth over 200,000 yuan. The canal is now releasing water again, and wheat seedlings are being widely planted, with the hope of a bumper harvest next year. The reason reported is that the culverts and sluices of the canal have been completely repaired, are sturdy and flexible, close when the water is low, and open when the water is high, so that droughts and floods are no longer a concern. The authorities advocate agricultural revitalization and benefit the people, and their merits are truly inconceivable.

Passengers who Declare Traveling Without a Ticket, etc., are Exempt from Fines 118

The Beijing-Shanghai and Shanghai-Hangzhou-Ningbo Railway Bureau received Training Order No. 337 from the Ministry of Railways, stating: "According to the Business Department's submission of a letter from the Traffic Department of the Beijing-Shanghai and Shanghai-Hangzhou-Ningbo Railway, regarding the issuance of Training Order No. 2610 from the ministry, instructing to revise the regulations on supplementary tickets and fines, and to amend Article 47, paragraph 1, of the Passenger Transport Regulations, etc." After approval, they were instructed to comply. "However, Article 47 of the regulations stipulates that passengers who travel beyond their station or class, if they declare in advance, may be exempt from fines. Does this measure still apply? Also, for passengers traveling without a ticket, in addition to paying the fare, are the fines not waived regardless of the reason? As the interpretation of the regulations is concerned, this department does not dare to act on its own," etc. After review, the ministry's amendment of Article 47 of the Passenger Transport Regulations refers to paragraph 1. The provisos in Items 2 and 3 of paragraph 1 have not been amended. Therefore, the measure of exempting passengers who declare in advance from punishment for traveling beyond their station or class still applies. As for whether fines for passengers traveling without a ticket should not be waived regardless of the reason, since the original article had no proviso, fines should not be waived in any case. However, it has been found that some passengers traveling without a ticket do not have enough time to buy a ticket before the train departs. It does not seem fair not to provide for a waiver in such cases. Therefore, the provisos in Items 2 and 3 of paragraph 1 of the above article are deleted, and the proviso is amended so that all three situations can be applied. The amended wording is as follows: (1) Traveling without a ticket, (2) traveling beyond the station, (3) traveling beyond the class. However, passengers in the above three situations who declare to the conductor or ticket inspector when boarding the train or before traveling beyond the station or class may be exempt from paying additional fines. In addition to separate orders, you are instructed to comply. This is an order.

Fish Market Workers to Adopt Employment System 119

Hoping to Avoid the Abuses of the Contracting System

The Shanghai Fish Market building project of the Ministry of Industries is nearing completion, and various preparations are actively underway. This has been reported in previous issues. The handling of fish differs from ordinary goods, and the method of worker management that would be both efficient and free of corruption is also a question. Yesterday, a reporter from the Central News Agency met with a member of the Preparatory Committee of the market and inquired whether a decision had been made. The committee member stated responsibly that the issue of dockworker management had been discussed multiple times in the Standing Committee meeting. Considering the many abuses inherent in the contracting system, it was decided not to adopt it. Instead, workers will be hired directly by the market to avoid exploitation by contractors, allowing laborers to receive their full earnings. Furthermore, considering that some dockworkers from fish businesses may face unemployment, priority will be given to hiring them to ensure a skilled workforce. The specific methods of hiring and management are currently being planned in consultation between the Ministry and the Central People’s Movement Guidance Committee. Recently, there have been reports of unscrupulous individuals falsely claiming affiliation to deceive and swindle others. The Committee is determined to investigate such matters, and assistance from all sectors is requested to report any such incidents to the Committee. Finally, it is reiterated that the fish market was established with the approval of the Central Political Conference, following a proposal by the Ministry of Industries. The Ministry allocated 500,000 yuan in official start-up funds as a national investment. Additional funding was also provided as a loan from the Ministry of Industries. Recent reports in some newspapers stating that the funds were temporarily advanced by the National Economic Council are not accurate.

Municipal Zoo Displays Giant Whale Specimen Yesterday 121

Visitors From All Sectors Show Great Enthusiasm. South African Exotic Fish to be Displayed Soon.

The giant whale specimen at the Municipal Zoo has been completed and was displayed starting yesterday morning for public viewing. Several species of small exotic fish from South Africa will be displayed after the specimen room is prepared. The details are as follows:

Giant Whale Display

To enhance public knowledge, the Municipal Zoo collected a giant whale previously discovered on the Chongming beach. After being transported back to Shanghai, the process of creating a specimen began. The whale specimen is over three zhang (approximately 10 meters) long, seven to eight chi (approximately 2.3-2.7 meters) high, and has a circumference of over one zhang. Six civilian houses were acquired to display the giant whale, and after construction was completed, the specimen was opened to the public yesterday morning. An entrance fee is charged, but no other fees are collected.

South African Exotic Fish

The zoo recently collected several species of small exotic fish from South Africa, placing them in glass tanks. These include four zebra fish, one “door fish” (said to engage in fierce battles when placed with other male fighting fish), one glass fish (whose entire skeleton, brain, and stomach are transparent), and five or six “trailer beard” fish. These will be displayed to the public after the specimen room is prepared.

Elephant Enclosure Construction

The zoo previously purchased an elephant from India. Since its arrival in Shanghai, the elephant has been temporarily housed in a bamboo enclosure because the elephant enclosure had not been built. This arrangement has proven inconvenient for visitors. The zoo has obtained approval from the Municipal Education Bureau to allocate funds for the construction of an elephant enclosure at a suitable location. Construction has begun, using iron bars all around and a cement roof, making it extremely sturdy. It is expected to be completed by the middle of the month.

Shanghai Dredging Bureau is Recruiting a Chinese Captain for its Dredger 122

The Dredging Bureau seeks a Chinese captain for its mud dredging vessel

The Shanghai Dredging Bureau, in order to dredge the Yangtze River mouth shoal (i.e. Jisha) outside of the Wusongkou, ordered a giant automatic mud-dredging vessel from the Schichau iron factory in Germany. Since its arrival in China for testing, it has been four months and the vessel has performed excellently in its various functions. The vessel's captain was previously dispatched by the Schichau iron factory during the testing period, so that he would be familiar with the vessel's machinery. It has now been heard that the captain's contract is about to expire, and the Dredging Bureau has decided to hire a Chinese captain to captain the giant (Construction) vessel. Yesterday, a notice was issued stating that candidates must have the following qualifications: (1) a fully qualified Class A captain's certificate; (2) a thorough understanding of the general conditions of the Yangtze River estuary; (3) the ability to operate the vessel during dredging operations, and possess exceptional piloting skills and experience; and (4) be no more than 45 years of age. The salary during the probationary period is set at 50 British pounds, plus 60 yuan for housing. Applicants with the above skills should submit their applications to the Bureau before October 24th, pending a scheduled examination.

It will arrive in Tai'an on the morning of the 11th, spending the whole day on the mountain, departing at 11:00 PM that night. It will arrive in Qufu on the morning of the 12th, touring the Confucius Forest and Confucius Temple, departing at 7:00 PM that afternoon. It will arrive in Chuzhou on the morning of the 13th, touring Langya Temple, Zuiweng Pavilion, and other places, departing at 7:00 PM that night. It will arrive in Shanghai at 7:15 AM on the 14th. This special train is a second-class sleeper car, providing bedding. Special staff will be assigned to guide the tour along the way and make travel arrangements for the guests. The round-trip fare includes the sleeper fee and the cost of meals on the train. The total cost is 42 yuan per person for those departing from Shanghai and 30 yuan per person for those departing from Nanjing. Two children may share one ticket and occupy one berth. One child will be charged the adult fare. The ticket sales period will end on the evening of October 7th for Beijing-Shanghai and on the evening of the 8th for Tianjin-Pukou. Tickets will be sold at: Tianjin-Pukou Railway Nanjing Sales Office, Beijing-Shanghai Railway Shanghai First Sales Office, and Second Sales Office. It is said that the number of tour tickets is limited to 90. Those who are interested in touring should purchase them as soon as possible to avoid disappointment.

Workers at the Zhabei Water and Electricity Plant Oppose Service Rules 126

Company Says They Will Await Authorities' Review

According to the Central News Agency, the workers at the Zhabei Water and Electricity Company have petitioned the Party and government authorities and made requests to the company due to their opposition to the worker service rules. This was reported in yesterday’s newspaper. A reporter visited the company yesterday and, according to the company, the workers’ representatives spoke with the deputy manager of the company the other day but did not put forward concrete opinions. As for the worker service rules, they were formulated according to the workers’ past service at the company, based on labor laws and local worker service rules, and were approved by the social affairs bureau and implemented on July 1st. It has been three months since then. The articles that the workers reportedly oppose, such as articles 23, 24, 49, and 52, etc., have no legitimate reason for opposition. A review of the articles will immediately reveal this. The provision in Article 14 is due to the fact that water and electricity are essential for residents’ daily use and local security, and cannot be interrupted day or night. If there is an obstacle, it should be repaired immediately and cannot be stopped outside of working hours. Also, when work is urgent and the original workers are insufficient or inadequate to handle it, it is unavoidable to have workers from other departments take on the responsibility temporarily. The company treats its staff in the same way, and it has been the practice for many years to give extra wages for temporary work outside of working hours. The workers have never expressed dissent, and it is unexpected that they are suddenly opposed. The company can only await the review of the relevant authorities. The articles of the service rules that the workers reportedly oppose are listed below: Article 14: Even though the company’s workers have stipulated working hours, the supervisor may summon them to work or order them to extend their working hours when necessary, and the workers may not refuse on the grounds of excuse. If a worker is instructed by a supervisor to take on other types of work temporarily during working hours, the worker may not refuse on the grounds of excuse. Article 23: Workers may not leave their posts without permission during working hours, or engage in activities that hinder the work of others, or read books, newspapers, or magazines, or talk, laugh, or play with others. Article 24: Workers may not linger in any of the company’s workplaces outside of working hours. Article 49: After a worker’s leave of absence expires, he or she should immediately return to the company to cancel the leave. If it is necessary to extend the leave, it is limited to one time, except in cases of illness, and may not exceed half of the original leave. Article 52: Workers may not request leave of absence during work hours, but this does not apply if there is an important incident that is proven to be true and has been approved by the supervisor.

Special District Rickshaw Guild Petitioned the Vehicle Committee Yesterday Morning 127

Requesting Re-Registration Due to Insufficient Rickshaw Pullers

The Special District Rickshaw Guild petitioned the Vehicle Committee yesterday morning regarding the registration of rickshaw pullers. Details are as follows:

Rickshaw Business Petition

The Special District Rickshaw Guild believed that the number of registered rickshaw pullers was too small, and in addition, pullers were continuously returning to their hometowns, leading to an insufficient supply. They held a meeting the night before and resolved to (1) send representatives Hou Shaoan, Lu Dexin, and others to petition the Vehicle Committee to re-register as much as possible; (2) send experts to conduct research on new rickshaw designs; (3) notify each rickshaw owner to separately compile and report the number of registered rickshaw pullers, the number of people who have returned to their hometowns or changed jobs, and submit them to the guild for discussion; (4) manage the vehicles, keep them clean and hygienic, and stay until midnight. Yesterday morning at 5:00 AM, petition representatives Hou Shaoan and Lu Dexin went to the Vehicle Committee to petition, where they were received by Wang Zhiren. Regarding the point of maximizing registration, he promised to submit it to the chairman for approval.

Notice to Rickshaw Owners

The guild issued a notice to all rickshaw owners stating that since the Public Works Bureau inspected rickshaw puller armbands on September 15th of this year, they have received a flood of letters from rickshaw owners, claiming that there were not enough rickshaw pullers, resulting in many vehicles being idled and business plummeting. If the rickshaw puller registration is not supplemented, it will inevitably lead to bankruptcy. Based on this, the office convened the 90th emergency meeting of the board of directors the other day, and decided to send representatives, including Mr. Hou Shaoan, to negotiate with the authorities. The authorities have now agreed to the request. However, each rickshaw owner must, within three days from the date of this announcement, compile the number of rickshaws owned, the number of registered rickshaw pullers, the number of people who have returned to their hometowns or changed jobs and have taken their armbands with them, and each item such as the names of the rickshaw pullers and the numbers of their armbands, and report them to the guild. This is so that a method can be negotiated to maximize the registration of rickshaw pullers, and to avoid the difficulties of "having vehicles but no pullers, and having pullers but no vehicles." This matter is closely related to the vital interests of rickshaw owners, the survival of their business, and the lives of rickshaw pullers, and is extremely important. It is hoped that each rickshaw owner will proceed quickly and conscientiously in accordance with the above-mentioned time frame and methods, and do not delay or delay, so as not to cause self-defeating. In addition to publishing notices in the Xin and Shen newspapers, special letters are sent separately as above.

Auditorium Arrangement

The auditorium arrangement is the same as in previous sessions. The wedding platform is decorated with red ribbons, with tall dragon and phoenix candles burning in front. Red silk banners are hung on both sides. In the center is the seating area for the wedding participants, arranged in an orderly fashion according to the magnetic tile numbers on the floor, with odd numbers on the left and even numbers on the right. A red carpet is laid in the hall, reaching straight to the door. A red silk banner is hung in front of the door, with the words "Shanghai Municipal Fourth Group Wedding Ceremony" written on it. The arrangement is quite luxurious and grand.

Wedding Ceremony

The wedding ceremony is extremely simple and solemn. (1) All wedding participants stand at attention; (2) Paying the highest respect to the national flag and the portrait of Dr. Sun Yat-sen: bow once, bow twice, bow thrice; (3) The officiant reads the wedding address; (4) The new couples bow to each other: bow once, bow twice; (5) The officiant presents the wedding certificates and souvenirs; (6) The officiant delivers an address; (7) All wedding participants bow to the officiant.

Broadcasting Ceremony

In order to enable the general public to understand the etiquette of group weddings, the municipal government will broadcast all wedding ceremonies, officiant's address, and wedding address to the city from the city broadcasting station at 2:00 PM today. The station's frequency is cooKC, with a power of 500 watts.

Yesterday's Rehearsal

Yesterday afternoon at 2:00 PM, a wedding ceremony rehearsal was first held at the Municipal Auditorium. It started at 2:15 PM. Municipal Secretary-General Yu Hongjun and Social Affairs Bureau Chief Wu Xingya both came to give guidance. Master of ceremonies Wang Xianqing, representing the officiant, reported the points that the new couples should pay attention to during today's ceremony, such as (1) standing neatly when facing each other; (2) paying attention to posture when receiving the certificate and stepping down from the stage; (3) walking slowly during the ceremony. All the wedding participants rehearsed according to the etiquette, which was quite orderly and skillful. It ended at 3:40 PM.

Chinese General Sales Corporation Has Appointed a Custodian 131

Mr. Walshiff Appointed Because He Has No Ties To Either Side

The Shanghai "The China Press" reported that Chief Judge Helmick of the U.S. Court for China issued an order on Monday afternoon appointing Mr. Walshiff, the general manager of Chinese General Sales Corporation, as the custodian of the company. The company had invoked U.S. bankruptcy law and petitioned the U.S. Court to appoint a custodian last week. The petition stated that the company's total assets exceeded its total liabilities, but it was unable to meet its maturing debts due to financial deficits and falling real estate prices. The company's real estate is worth more than 17 million yuan, but it has only 60,000 yuan in cash. It therefore requested the court to appoint a custodian to take over the assets and continue operations pending the formulation of a reorganization plan in accordance with U.S. bankruptcy law and approval by the court. Mr. Hickmick appointed Mr. Walshiff as the custodian of the company because he had recently arrived in Shanghai from the United States, had no ties to any party, and was fair-minded. He would continue to operate the company pending further orders, but he must submit a surety bond of US$50,000 as proof of faithful performance of his duties. The surety bond is reportedly to be filed today (Tuesday).

The "Ta Mei Wan Pao" reported that Mr. Walshiff's US$50,000 surety bond was filed today (the 1st). Mr. Walshiff stated today that the company will continue to operate as usual pending further orders from the U.S. Court.

Malaria is Rampant in Minhang; Municipal Council Issues Another Warning 139

Shanghai Residents Visiting Minhang Should Take Extra Precautions

The Health Department of the Municipal Council has previously issued a warning to the public through newspapers that dangerous malaria is prevalent in the Minhang area south of Shanghai. Travelers to Minhang should take extra precautions. They should stay behind screens or mosquito nets after dark to prevent mosquito bites or consult a doctor beforehand and take quinine or other mixtures for prevention. Now, according to a report from the Director of the Health Department, many villagers have recently been sent to the Municipal Council Inspection Office from the Minhang area by their relatives. They are all suffering from malignant tertian malaria. There are also foreign residents in the area who are infected. The Health Department is currently intensifying its investigation, and the report is not yet complete. The Director of the Health Department also stated that there is no malignant tertian malaria in Shanghai proper. This type of malaria is extremely difficult to treat, and patients often have difficulty recovering after the illness. Minhang is very close, and many people travel there, so in order to avoid infection and protect the safety of the city, it is hoped that those Shanghai residents who go to Minhang should follow the previous warning and take extra precautions to avoid causing trouble for themselves.

Assassination Case from Seven Years Ago; Two Masterminds Arrested 140

Public Security Bureau Requests Transfer; Court Orders Postponement for Further Hearing

Gu Da Gouzi, foreman of the British-owned Gongyi Yarn Factory at 150 Robison Road in Shanghai West, was shot and killed on Robison Road in August of the 17th year of the Republic of China. The case has been going on for seven years, and the murderer has not been caught. The night before last, Sha Daxin, captain of the Fourth Squad of the Municipal Public Security Bureau, learned that a suspect in the case, Yuan Aliang, was hiding at No. 14 Renrui Lane, Caojiadu. He then, together with the Sixth District Public Security Bureau, arrested Yuan. Yuan confessed that the masterminds were Zhao Chunquan and Zhao Bingquan, two local brothers who were the chief foremen of the Gongyi Yarn Factory. Their home is at No. 77 Ziyang Lane, 190 Wuding Road. Captain Sha then reported to the relevant Gordon Road Police Station at around 2:00 AM yesterday, and together with Chinese Detective Zhu Mengwei, arrested the two Zhaos and took them to the police station. At 5:30 AM, they were sent to the Eighth Criminal Court of the First Special Court. The Zhao brothers hired lawyer Chen Ru to represent them in court. The police lawyer Zhang Tianyin stated the case, saying that this case was an assistance case. When arresting Zhao Chunquan and Zhao Bingquan, the police found two pistols and two licenses. The two guns have now been sent to the Municipal Council Armory for inspection. Therefore, the case requests a postponement. The arrested Yuan Aliang confessed that he was 49 years old and had been a foreman in the Yisha Factory. He knew Zhao Chunquan and others. The deceased, Gu Da Gouzi, was also a foreman in the factory. On a certain day before his death, the Zhao brothers and Wang Xiaoxiazi, Ouyang, Yao Lu and others, who are still at large, discussed in a small room upstairs in the Gongyi Yarn Factory that Gu Xiaogouzi's work in the factory was quite unfavorable to them, so they planned to ask someone to take drastic action. At that time, I passed by the factory and happened to hear this. Later, I was dragged in by them, and so on. Moreover, Shua Dasheng and Shan Bin, the officers from the Public Security Bureau, applied to transfer the case. Zhao Chunquan confessed, saying that the deceased Gu Da Gouzi, Yuan Aliang and others were all foremen who were subordinate to me, and there was no enmity. What Yuan confessed was completely untrue. Judge Liu Yugui reviewed the confessions and ordered the two Zhaos to be detained and heard again in seven days.

Member of Defense Corps Killed Near Jiaotong Road 141

Yu Tianxiang, a member of the Fourth Squad of the Defense Corps in the Zhao Family Garden area near Zhongshan Road in Zhabei, a Henan native, about thirty years old, was assigned to serve at the Zhengfeng School on Jiaotong Road. This tragic incident is believed to be a vendetta. It is said that there were also many knife wounds on his head. Yu Guoying Seriously Injured by Knives

Mother Commits Suicide After Son is Arrested 143

How Can a Son Feel at Ease?

The French Concession Police Department discovered some sort of organization in the house at No. 3, Lane 268, Fulu Li Road in the French Concession some days ago. It sent Chinese and foreign detectives to search the premises. Zhu Xianzou, a native of Anhui who lived in the pavilion, was suspected and arrested for interrogation. Because no connection was found, he was released. However, Zhu never returned home. His old mother, surnamed Mou, about fifty years old, suddenly had a momentary thought. On the evening of the 30th of last month, she hanged herself with a hemp rope on the stairs when people were quiet at dusk. Yesterday morning at six o'clock, the rope she hanged herself with suddenly broke for some unknown reason, and the old woman's body rolled down the stairs with a loud noise. At this time, a detective assigned by the French Police Department to conduct a secret investigation happened to arrive at the door. Hearing the noise, he entered and saw that the old woman's body had rolled down to the bottom of the stairs. He felt that the body was already cold and reported to Zhang Daosheng, the local landlord who lived in the bungalow behind the house. Zhang Daosheng reported to the French Police Department, which sent detectives to carry the body to the Sijen Auxiliary Yuantang Corpse Inspection Office. Since there was no way to find her family, the Second Special Court was notified. Prosecutor Wang Ren and the forensic scribe arrived at the office and confirmed that Zhu Mou had indeed committed suicide by hanging. The body was handed over to the Tongren Auxiliary Yuantang for embalming and burial pending identification by her family.

Method for Calculating Freight for Baskets of Tea in Joint Transport 145

One-Year Trial to Begin on the 11th of This Month

The Joint Management Bureau of the Beijing-Shanghai and Shanghai-Hangzhou-Ningbo Railways received instructions from the Ministry of Railways yesterday, roughly stating that for all joint transport routes, the method of calculating freight for baskets of tea based on special light and bulky goods, using four cubic decimeters as one kilogram, should be implemented uniformly on all joint transport routes to attract business. The trial will begin on October 11th of this year for a period of one year. Tobacco Leaf Association Writes to the Municipal Chamber of Commerce, Requesting Leadership to Protect National Livelihood 146

The Tobacco Leaf Industry Association sent a letter to the Municipal Chamber of Commerce, stating: "We respectfully inform you that members of our association and cigarette manufacturers often go to Henan Province to purchase tobacco leaves, and Xuchang is the place where tobacco leaves are concentrated. The British American Tobacco Company in this city, in the past, under the name of its liaison Ren Boyan, established a tobacco leaf factory there to purchase tobacco leaves at low prices, process them, and sell them. The quantity was very large. As a foreign company infringing on domestic rights and interests, violating agreements, and manipulating and oppressing, it has long been criticized by the Chinese people. Fortunately, the provincial authorities discovered this and immediately ordered the factory to stop operating, which was applauded by the people. Later, all sectors of Xuchang, fearing that foreign economic aggression might reignite, jointly requested the government to abolish the tobacco factory base and return it to the local government for the construction of schools or hospitals to prevent future troubles. However, the matter was about to be completed when Shi Kunshan, a staff member at the time, sold it to the Xuchang Company on behalf of the company. Upon investigation, although the Xuchang Company is ostensibly organized by the Chinese Wu Tingsheng, it is still affiliated with the British American Tobacco Company behind the scenes, merely using this to avoid the attention of our government and people. Now, we have learned that their plan is to transfer the tobacco factory base to the Yu-Su Curing Tobacco Factory after it is purchased by the Xuchang Company. On the one hand, they will mortgage the property to the British American Tobacco Company. In one transfer, the economic power will still be taken over by foreigners. Now, Niu Siming, an American who has been working for the British American Tobacco Company for more than ten years, has been introduced by Wu Tingsheng to serve as the technical advisor and general manager of the Yu-Su Curing Tobacco Factory. He has also used this position to appoint six foreigners from the company to various key positions. Preparations have been fully completed and all of this has been created by Wu Tingsheng. Anyone with blood in their veins despises such people who willingly pander to foreigners and act as accomplices, disregarding the suffering of the people. The factory is currently actively proceeding. Once realized, the tobacco leaves produced in the province will surely be completely taken over by them. Not only will the tobacco farmers be oppressed, and their suffering will be endless, but also more than 300,000 people in the producing areas and the ports of Beijing, Tianjin, Shanghai, and Hankou who depend on this industry for their livelihoods will become unemployed. Chinese cigarette factories will also be hit. The damage is extremely serious. The matter concerns collusion with foreigners to invade domestic rights and interests and harm people's livelihoods. All Chinese people should unanimously condemn it. The members of our association feel deeply and cannot remain silent. Therefore, we are writing this letter to earnestly request that your association, considering that the matter concerns the livelihoods of hundreds of thousands of people, quickly take the lead in thoroughly explaining the pros and cons, and conveying them to the authorities. We earnestly request that you strictly order your subordinates to make every effort to stop it, so as to avoid causing harm to the local area and protect the livelihoods of the people. We are extremely grateful." It is reported that the Municipal Chamber of Commerce has reported the situation to the Ministry of Finance and the Ministry of Industry and is requesting that they issue orders to stop it in order to protect the livelihoods of the Chinese people.

Invented a Pressure Oil Lamp that Burns Domestic Oil 152

Bright Light, Convenient Burning, Ministry of Industry Approves Patent for Sale

Available for Sale in One Month

Crude oil is one of the major import commodities of our country. In places where there are no electric lights in the interior, almost all kerosene lamps are used. Mr. Zhong Ling, the owner of the Hanli Company on Shandong Road in this city, who is also the inventor of the Zhongling Printing Machine, in order to stop the waste, researched with his friend Liao Fuya for two years and invented a pressure oil lamp. The lamp can burn domestic oil such as domestic rapeseed oil, soybean oil, and cottonseed oil. Because of the internal structure of the lamp, there is elastic pressure, which can keep the oil and wick level. The lamp is convenient to burn and emits bright light, which is enough to rival kerosene lamps. After the lamp was invented, it was tested and approved by the Ministry of Industry, and a patent was granted for its sale. The lamp will be available in about a month. The factory is currently located on Huade Road, Jingzhou Road for manufacturing. It is heard that there are more than ten types of lamps, and it is also learned that each lamp costs from a few cents to over one yuan. It is a truly cheap and good product and a powerful weapon for recovering rights and interests.

Verdict in the Fei Family Internal Dispute Case 155

Fei Yusheng and Others Exempted from Punishment

Fei Keming, a real estate tycoon with assets of several tens of thousands, recently passed away due to illness. Before even 100 days had passed, his children were already fighting amongst themselves over inheritance rights. Initially, the eldest son, Yusheng, reported to the police that his younger brother, Junwen, had seized the ancestral tablet and obstructed the funeral. After the police initiated legal proceedings, Huang Junwen was sentenced to two months of imprisonment with a suspended sentence. Now, Junwen's wife, Huang, has also reported to the police that her elder brother-in-law, Fei Yusheng, his son, Qigang, and the wife of her younger uncle-in-law, Meiwen, Ms. Yang, had jointly caused her injury. The police, in accordance with the law, also filed charges. The police lawyer, Qian Xunjiu, prosecuted them in the First Special District Court on charges of assault. After a round of questioning, the details of which have been recorded in this newspaper, Judge Dai Rongduo of the Second Criminal Court continued the hearing yesterday morning and announced the verdict: Fei Yusheng and Fei Qigang were exempted from punishment for jointly causing bodily harm; Fei Yang was found not guilty. Police lawyer Qian declared that he would waive the right to appeal. After the verdict, Judge Dai addressed both parties, saying that since they were all compatriots, they should not discriminate against each other. Therefore, Fei Yusheng and Fei Qigang were given suspended sentences, in the hope that both sides would reconcile and cooperate, and not engage in further internal strife. Both parties respectfully agreed and left. This internal family feud case has thus come to an end.

Trial Record of Ren Linggui vs. Qian Guocheng 158

Qian Guocheng from Beijing, who previously worked at a company in this city, became severely ill in the spring of this year and was hospitalized for more than two months before being discharged. His body and spirit were both in pain, and Qian lost his job as a result. In July, he hired three lawyers, Su Fuchou, Li Mo, and Yan Hongxi, and filed a lawsuit with the Second Special Court, citing the crime of injury under criminal law, and also attached a civil claim demanding compensation for losses and expenses totaling 5,520 yuan. The defendants were the president of the hospital, Yan Fuqing, the vice president, Liu Chongen, and the chief of surgery, Ren Linggui. The Second Special Court held that the evidence of Qian being burned was indeed true, but the person who directly burned Qian was not Ren Linggui, so the crime could not be established. In early September, the court pronounced him not guilty. Recently, Ren Linggui sued Qian for false accusation. Yesterday (October 1st) at 9:30 AM, the Third Criminal Court convened and summoned both parties for questioning. After Ren Linggui testified, Qian Guocheng testified, stating that when he was sick and went to the hospital in the spring, he personally saw Ren Linggui and Dr. Ji Changgeng both present. Later, because he was under anesthesia, he lost consciousness and could not say who performed the surgery. However, since Ren Linggui was the chief of surgery, he could not shirk responsibility, so he sued him last time. At this point, Qian presented his feet in court, showing red scars. The lawyer then made a statement, but since the defendant's lawyer had not arrived, Qian defended himself. Subsequently, Prosecutor Chen Shu expressed his opinion, stating that Ren Linggui was the chief of surgery, and Qian Guocheng had not known Ren Linggui before and had no feud with him, so it was not a false accusation. Judge Wang Cheng announced the conclusion of the debate and set the verdict for 9:00 AM on the 8th of this month.

Letters 164

To the Editor: We are writing to address a recent report in your newspaper's local news section regarding a theft case. The report stated that "Cheng Wenjun (also known as Wang Wenjun)" is a female performer in our company and that on September 11th, she introduced her husband, Ji Jinsheng, to also become a performer in our company, and that they went to Hangzhou on the same day to film a movie, returning on the 17th. We find this information quite perplexing. Upon investigation, we have found that there are no performers named Cheng or Ji in our company's roster. Moreover, there have been no film shoots in Hangzhou in recent months. The statements made by the criminals Ji and Cheng are clearly false. In addition to instructing our lawyer to request a thorough investigation by the court, we are clarifying the facts to ensure that your esteemed newspaper's accurate reporting is not misled by false information. We would be grateful if you could publish this letter as a correction. Sincerely, Shanghai Diantong Company, October 1st. Respectfully,

To the Editor: We are writing to address a report published on page 3 of your newspaper's local news section on September 30th, titled "How a Ship's Mate Drowned, Police Station Sends for Investigation". The report does not align with the facts. According to the report from the Yangsi sub-station, the incident occurred on the afternoon of September 19th. The deceased's brother, Yao Yinhai, reported the incident to the Yang Rengang outpost of the Third Division of the Water Patrol Team, who summoned the ship owner, Gong Haigen, for questioning and transferred him to the General Team, who then transferred him to the Public Security Bureau for investigation. The Water Patrol Team also ordered the local bailiff, Zhao Ketang, to report to the Shanghai Local Court, who sent personnel on the 21st to conduct an inspection and confirmed that the death was due to drowning. A notice of burial was issued. On the afternoon of the 25th at 3:00 PM, according to reports from Weng Maoxiong and Zhang Bocai, the deceased's aunt, Zhang Yao, went to Gong Haigen's home to argue, and was beaten and injured by Haigen's wife. We asked the plaintiff for details, but she only shook her head and remained silent. We immediately dispatched police and ordered the defendant to appear, but they were evading. However, since the plaintiff was over seventy years old, we sent her to the hospital for treatment first. Furthermore, on the 28th, the deceased's wife, Yao Jiang, father, Yao Boting, and brother, Yao Yinhai, went to Gong Haigen's home to demand wages and discuss matters related to the deceased's funeral, causing a disturbance. Gong Haigen's mother, Sun, along with the local bailiff Zhao Ketang, reported to the sub-station, who summoned them for mediation. Long Sun paid Yao Yinhai 17 yuan to settle the wage dispute. As for the matters related to the deceased's funeral, since a lawsuit has been filed with the court, all parties should await the court's decision. However, our station did not conduct any investigation or make any other statements regarding this case. The information in the report is likely based on rumors and is inaccurate. We are writing to request a correction to prevent any confusion. Sincerely, Tang Qiao Police Station, Pudong Branch of the Shanghai Municipal Public Security Bureau, October 1st. Respectfully,

To the Editor: We are writing to address a report in your newspaper today regarding news of a martial arts group performing to aid disaster relief. There are a few points that do not align with the facts. (1) The Martial Arts Disaster Relief Performance, held on September 28th and 29th, was initiated by the Shanghai Martial Arts Hall and the Jingwu Athletic Association, along with 27 other organizations. The event initiated by Mr. Yang Guangshang is a separate organization and has no connection to the organizations mentioned in your report. (2) The event only lasted for two days, September 28th and 29th, and has already concluded. We are writing to request a correction. Sincerely, Shanghai Martial Arts Hall, October 1st.

A Glimpse of Their Strength

Sichuan Province participated in the 4th National Games in 1931 for the first time, with only ten athletes, all students from Chengdu University and Normal University. The second time was in 1933 for the 5th National Games, with one hundred and twenty athletes, organized by the 20th Army of Sichuan. This year, due to limited funding, there are only sixty-seven athletes, organized by the Sichuan Provincial Government, marking the first legally generated Sichuan National Games team. They are participating in seven events for the men's group: track and field, all-around, football, volleyball, tennis, and martial arts, and three events for the women's group: track and field, basketball, and tennis. Among them, male tennis players Wang Wenzhi and Qian Yaobin, and female tennis players Li Yuping and Ye Yuru, are all strong and will compete with Shanghai, Java, Hong Kong, and Shanxi. In track and field, female high jumper Pang Lu has a height of 1.6 meters, and male all-around athlete Kuang Nengwen has a score of 40 points, both of which have hopes of scoring.

Team Leader's Statement

According to the team leader Liu Shenzhan, the team had a total of eighty-five male and female athletes during the preliminary selections. Since August 15th, they have undergone more than four weeks of rigorous training and selection, eliminating those with poor progress, unqualified qualifications, or bad habits. Now the team has a total of sixty-seven people. After arriving in Shanghai, each athlete will continue to be strictly managed according to the training period, and their diet, daily life, and various exercises will be on a fixed schedule, without interruption, in order to win glory for Sichuan during the National Games.

The City Swimming Pool Shines Brightly Last Night: A Record of the Hong Kong-Shanghai Swimming Performance 172

Liang Weisheng's 100-Meter Performance is Comparatively Beautiful; Women's Team Sweeps All, Performance is Quite Spectacular; Tonight, Hong Kong-Shanghai Joint Team Competes Against Westerners

The first act of the Sino-Western Swimming Competition, hosted by the City Swimming Pool, the first Hong Kong-Shanghai Intercity Competition, opened at the City Hall's new pool last night at 8:00 PM. Both teams are authorities in the swimming world, especially with the widespread fame of the mermaid, attracting a large crowd on Jiangwan Road. The total number of spectators was no less than a thousand. Unfortunately, there was a light rain around 7:00 PM, which became heavier, otherwise there would have been over five thousand people. The City Pool added two new floodlights the day before, making it even more magnificent. Wu Tiecheng, the mayor and chairman of the competition, along with honorary referees Li Chao, Pan Gongzhan, Jing Lun, and others, arrived at the venue around 8:10 PM and watched the competition by the pool. The entire program had eleven events, with four performances and seven official events. The Hong Kong team swept the women's events, while the Shanghai team won three out of the five men's events. Liang Weisheng also set a new city record in the 100-meter freestyle. Details are as follows:

General Overview of the Men's Group

At 8:00 PM, the rain was still drizzling. By the time the competition started, it had stopped. The first event was the men's 50-meter freestyle. Hong Kong's star Chen Zhenxing was unable to participate due to his lack of training. Shanghai's Xu Heng took the lead with an excellent start, finishing about two inches ahead of Li Luomin. The others were difficult to distinguish. Liang Weisheng focused on the 100-meter event and gave up this event, otherwise, with his score of 18.9 seconds, he would have dominated the competition. When the 100-meter freestyle started, Liang looked calm and focused. After diving into the water, he quickly surpassed the others, leading the pack. He finished with a time of one minute and 7.8 seconds, which was very beautiful and close to the national record. He finished eight meters ahead of the third-place finisher. It was a pity that Chen Zhenxing was not present, otherwise, there would have been a better record. In the 100-meter breaststroke, Jian Erjie was unable to participate due to tonsillitis. Zhong Shoujun edged out Hong Kong's Zeng Hefu by half a foot. Jian Erlian lost his position due to a mistake during the turn. In the 100-meter backstroke, Shanghai's Wei Guorui had not fully recovered from his illness and was not able to swim at his best. In the relay race, Shanghai's Xu Shouqiang swam first, but was passed by Hong Kong's Chen Qiqian. Although Jian Erming tried to catch up in the breaststroke, he was unable to close the gap. In the third leg, the Hong Kong team sent Chen Zhenxing, while Shanghai sent Liang. After diving into the water, Liang was a foot behind. They fought fiercely in the middle, but Chen gained a slight lead and won by a foot.

Women's and Performances

The Shanghai team did not win any of the three women's events, which were all won by the Hong Kong team. The mermaid's skill was truly extraordinary, attracting attention. In the 50-meter freestyle, she finished six feet ahead of her sister Xiuzhen, causing shouts and thunderous applause. In the 100-meter breaststroke, Hong Kong's Qu Enzhao was only thirteen years old, but she stood out after diving into the water. Shanghai's Zhou Xiuling tried her best to catch up, but was eleven feet behind. In the 100-meter freestyle, Shanghai's Zhu, the Yang sisters were still neck and neck before the turn, but the mermaid, who was skilled in both, swam faster and faster, finishing six feet ahead of her sister, while Chen fell behind Xiuzhen by three or four feet. The four performances were the highlight of the event. When the mermaid performed the windmill swimming, the audience erupted in applause. After diving into the water, she swam in a circle, her hands and body moving like a windmill, and the water swirled like a vortex. Chen Zhenxing's butterfly stroke was the latest American breaststroke style, with both hands thrusting forward simultaneously, the body slightly inclined, and the feet vertical, which increased the speed compared to the old style. In the diving performance, although it was fifty meters away, Chen Zhenxing Hong Erming's performance was impressive. Most people can only dive up to ten meters, but Chen had the ability and speed, and his posture was also excellent. Jian's central performance was slightly inferior. The last act was diving, which was also quite interesting.

Sino-Western Confrontation Tonight

Tonight is the Hong Kong-Shanghai Joint Team vs. Shanghai Westerners, starting at 8:30 PM. The program includes ten events: (1) Men's 50-meter freestyle: Watt, Bolideng, Pan Kaishuo, Chen Zhenxing, Li Luomin, Xu Heng; (2) Men's 100-meter breaststroke: Wheeler, Laiwu, Laimugen, Jian Erjie, Jian Erlian, Wu Gansheng; (3) Women's 100-meter freestyle: Tang Posheng, Mac Ligan, Yang Xiuqiong Yang Xiuzhen, Chen Yuhui; (4) Men's 100-meter backstroke: Kang Jiang Beilunzi, Chen Minqian, Foruiqin, Xu Shouqiang; (5) Men's 100-meter freestyle: Klik, Si Rike Si, Bailina, Chen Zhenxing, Liang Weisheng, Li Luomin; (6) Women's 50-meter breaststroke: Tang Bosheng, Mac Ligeng, Qu Sizhao, Zhou Suling, He Wenjing Zhang Jiazhen; (7) Men's fancy diving: Hengbo, Kai Er Keke Lai'er, Xu Xuanrui, Liang Guoquan, Yu Xunshi; (8) Comic diving: Mu, Lun Tuo, Qinsheng; (9) Men's 100-meter relay: Western Union Bolideng, Watt, Si Dai Tong Si Kai Pan Kaituo, Chinese Union Chen Zhenxing, Li Luomin, Liang Weisheng, Zeng Hefu; (10) Men's water polo match: Referee Mac Ligai, Timer Liang Zhaoan, Western Union Team Weijiang, Pan Qituo, Maimugen, Pike, Laimu, Ke Dan Ke Si, Watt, Chinese Union Team Zhou Dayun, Zhou Ruiqin, Chen Zhenxing, Zeng Afu, Chen Ziqing, Li Luomin, Zhang Rongguang.

Beijing-Shanghai Railway Bureau Issues Fixed-Period Train Tickets for the All-China Games 177

According to reliable sources, the Beijing-Shanghai Railway, in order to benefit spectators of the All-China Games, in addition to reducing the ticket price for the Sanmin Road branch line, has now printed several types of fixed-period train tickets. The fare from Baoshan Road to Sanmin Road Station is 2 yuan per ticket, and from Tiantong'an Station to Sanmin Road Station is 1.5 yuan per ticket. Both are valid for 11 days, from the opening day of the All-China Games to the closing day. Passengers who purchase these tickets can take the train to and from the All-China Games venue at any time, which is much cheaper than purchasing individual tickets. These fixed-period train tickets will be on sale starting October 5th.

Little Men (63) 191

— Original work by Ms. Alcott of the United States, translated by Zheng Xiaocang

Dan sneered at their boring views, and cursed even more fiercely as he taught them new games all the way.

However, Tommy was still drowsy, and Ned gradually felt a headache from the effects of the beer and cigarettes, so no one was in the mood to learn, and the card game was not exciting. The light was dim, and the room was almost dark. They couldn't laugh loudly, and they couldn't encourage each other much, because Mr. Rice was sleeping in the closet next door, so everyone was lazy and couldn't cheer up. Once, while dealing cards, Dan suddenly stopped and shouted, "Who is it?" His voice showed a frightened expression, and at the same time, he used his military cloak to cover the light. In the darkness, a voice trembled, "I can't find Tommy," followed by a rush of footsteps, from that main room to the side room.

"It's Jo! He's going to call someone; shrink into the bed immediately, Tommy, and don't say anything." Dan shouted, and quickly erased all traces of the fun just now, and began to quickly take off his clothes, as did Ned.

Tommy ran to his room like a fly, and slipped into his bed in a flash, so he just lay there smiling until his hand felt burning, only to find that he was still pinching the butt of the beautiful cigar. It turned out that they were still smoking when the happy gathering was dispersed.

The butt of the cigar was almost burned out, but he still wanted to carefully extinguish it. Suddenly, he heard Aunt Su's voice, and he was afraid that if he put it in the bed, his secret would be revealed, so he pinched it, thinking that he had finished it, and threw it under the bed.

Aunt Su came in, followed by Jo. She was surprised to see Tommy lying quietly, but his face was red. Jo asked him:

"He wasn't there just now, I woke up, and I couldn't find him anywhere."

Aunt Su shook his body lightly and asked, "What are you up to, you bad child?" This made the person lying down open his eyes and say gently:

"I just ran to Ned's room to ask him some questions. Go away, don't nag me, I'm going to sleep."

After Aunt Su helped Jo sleep well, she went to inspect again, and saw two children sleeping peacefully in Dan's room. "Some little games," she thought, and since she didn't see anything wrong, she didn't tell Mrs. Fife, who was busy taking care of little Todd and was already feeling annoyed.

Tommy was really sleepy. He only told Jo not to interfere and not to nag anymore. Later, he was snoring loudly in less than ten minutes, never dreaming of what had happened under his bed. It turned out that the cigar had not been extinguished, but was only smoldering on the straw mat. Later, it actually caught fire. So this hungry little flame crawled up like a snake, first caught the quilt, then gradually reached the bedding, and finally the bed itself caught fire. The beer made Tommy sleep very soundly, and the smoke suffocated Jo, so they fell asleep until the fire burned their bodies, and they were in danger of being burned to death.
